verification system is implemented across multiple Go files in the grafana/grafana repository. The system performs three main functions: plugin manifest signing verification, signature validation on load, and unsigned plugin allowlist enforcement.\\n\\n**Plugin Manifest Signing:**\\nThe `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go` file implements the core manifest signing logic. The `Calculate()` function reads the plugin's MANIFEST.txt file via `ReadPluginManifestFromFS()`, which opens and parses the PGP-signed manifest. The `validateManifest()` function validates all required manifest fields including manifestVersion, signatureType, signedByOrg, and keyId. The `Verify()` function performs cryptographic verification of the PGP signature using the OpenPGP library with public keys retrieved from a KeyRetriever. The manifest structure is defined as `PluginManifest` type which contains JSON fields including manifestVersion, signatureType, signedByOrg, signedByOrgName, and a map of file hashes.\\n\\n**File Integrity Verification:**\\nThe `verifyHash()` function in manifest.go validates that each file listed in the manifest matches its SHA256 hash. This ensures plugins haven't been modified. The function compares computed file checksums against the manifest's file map. Additional validation checks ensure the manifest version matches the plugin version and ID, verifying that signature metadata corresponds to the correct plugin.\\n\\n**Signature Validation on Load:**\\nThe validation pipeline is orchestrated through the bootstrap and validation stages. In `pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`, the `DefaultConstructor.Construct()` function calls `signatureCalculator.Calculate()` during the construct step of plugin loading. This calculates the plugin's initial signature state before validation.\\n\\nThe validation stage implements signature checking through `pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/steps.go` via the `SignatureValidationStep()` function which creates a `PluginSignatureValidator`. This validator calls the `ValidateSignature()` method from `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go`.\\n\\nThe core validation logic in `signature.go`'s `ValidateSignature()` function checks the plugin's signature status. It handles valid signatures (returns nil), invalid signatures (returns error), modified signatures (returns error), and unsigned plugins. For nested plugins, it optionally inherits the signature status from parent plugins. For unsigned plugins, it delegates to the authorizer's `CanLoadPlugin()` method.\\n\\n**Unsigned Plugin Allowlist Enforcement:**\\nThe `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go` file implements the `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` type with the `CanLoadPlugin()` method. This method enforces the allowlist by:\\n1. Returning true for any non-unsigned plugins\\n2. Returning true if dev mode is enabled\\n3. Checking if the plugin ID is in the `PluginsAllowUnsigned` configuration list\\n4. Returning false otherwise, blocking unsigned plugins not in the allowlist\\n\\nThe authorizer is instantiated via `NewUnsignedAuthorizer()` which wraps the PluginManagementCfg containing the allowlist configuration read from the `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` setting.\\n\\n**Public Key Retrieval:**\\nPlugin signature verification uses public keys provided by two sources:\\n\\n1. **Static Keys:** `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go` provides a hardcoded Grafana Labs public key embedded in the binary. The `KeyRetriever.GetPublicKey()` function returns this key when the key ID matches.\\n\\n2. **Dynamic Keys:** `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go` retrieves public keys from the Grafana API. The `GetPublicKey()` function queries a KV store cache. The `updateKeys()` function syncs keys with the Grafana API (/plugins/ci/keys endpoint) with a 10-day TTL. The service uses `ProvideService()` to instantiate either dynamic or static key retrieval based on configuration.\\n\\n**Service Integration:**\\nThe keyretriever service wrapper in `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go` provides a unified interface that coordinates between dynamic and static key retrieval. verification system is implemented across multiple Go files in the grafana/grafana repository. The system performs three main functions: plugin manifest signing verification, signature validation on load, and unsigned plugin allowlist enforcement.\\n\\n**Plugin Manifest Signing:**\\nThe `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go` file implements the core manifest signing logic. The `Calculate()` function reads the plugin's MANIFEST.txt file via `ReadPluginManifestFromFS()`, which opens and parses the PGP-signed manifest. The `validateManifest()` function validates all required manifest fields including manifestVersion, signatureType, signedByOrg, and keyId. The `Verify()` function performs cryptographic verification of the PGP signature using the OpenPGP library with public keys retrieved from a KeyRetriever. The manifest structure is defined as `PluginManifest` type which contains JSON fields including manifestVersion, signatureType, signedByOrg, signedByOrgName, and a map of file hashes.\\n\\n**File Integrity Verification:**\\nThe `verifyHash()` function in manifest.go validates that each file listed in the manifest matches its SHA256 hash. This ensures plugins haven't been modified. The function compares computed file checksums against the manifest's file map. Additional validation checks ensure the manifest version matches the plugin version and ID, verifying that signature metadata corresponds to the correct plugin.\\n\\n**Signature Validation on Load:**\\nThe validation pipeline is orchestrated through the bootstrap and validation stages. In `pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`, the `DefaultConstructor.Construct()` function calls `signatureCalculator.Calculate()` during the construct step of plugin loading. This calculates the plugin's initial signature state before validation.\\n\\nThe validation stage implements signature checking through `pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/steps.go` via the `SignatureValidationStep()` function which creates a `PluginSignatureValidator`. This validator calls the `ValidateSignature()` method from `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go`.\\n\\nThe core validation logic in `signature.go`'s `ValidateSignature()` function checks the plugin's signature status. It handles valid signatures (returns nil), invalid signatures (returns error), modified signatures (returns error), and unsigned plugins. For nested plugins, it optionally inherits the signature status from parent plugins. For unsigned plugins, it delegates to the authorizer's `CanLoadPlugin()` method.\\n\\n**Unsigned Plugin Allowlist Enforcement:**\\nThe `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go` file implements the `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` type with the `CanLoadPlugin()` method. This method enforces the allowlist by:\\n1. Returning true for any non-unsigned plugins\\n2. Returning true if dev mode is enabled\\n3. Checking if the plugin ID is in the `PluginsAllowUnsigned` configuration list\\n4. Returning false otherwise, blocking unsigned plugins not in the allowlist\\n\\nThe authorizer is instantiated via `NewUnsignedAuthorizer()` which wraps the PluginManagementCfg containing the allowlist configuration read from the `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` setting.\\n\\n**Public Key Retrieval:**\\nPlugin signature verification uses public keys provided by two sources:\\n\\n1. **Static Keys:** `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go` provides a hardcoded Grafana Labs public key embedded in the binary. The `KeyRetriever.GetPublicKey()` function returns this key when the key ID matches.\\n\\n2. **Dynamic Keys:** `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go` retrieves public keys from the Grafana API. The `GetPublicKey()` function queries a KV store cache. The `updateKeys()` function syncs keys with the Grafana API (/plugins/ci/keys endpoint) with a 10-day TTL. The service uses `ProvideService()` to instantiate either dynamic or static key retrieval based on configuration.\\n\\n**Service Integration:**\\nThe keyretriever service wrapper in `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go` provides a unified interface that coordinates between dynamic and static key retrieval. The `ProvideService()` function checks if dynamic key retrieval is disabled via `IsDisabled()` and falls back to static keys accordingly.\\n\\nAdditional validation layer in `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/steps.go` implements `SignatureValidationStep()` and `SignatureValidation.Validate()` which wraps the core signature validator and records errors for plugins with signature issues.\\n\\n**Data Structures:**\\nThe `pkg/plugins/models.go` file defines the core signature types: `Signature` struct with Status, Type, and SigningOrg fields; `SignatureStatus` type for states like valid, invalid, unsigned, modified, and internal; and `SignatureType` type for signature levels like grafana, community, and private.\\n\\nThe complete flow: Plugin discovery → Bootstrap stage (Calculate signature via manifest validation) → Validation stage (ValidateSignature with allowlist check) → Initialization stage. This pipeline architecture ensures plugins are validated before being made available to Grafana's frontend and backend systems.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
